PREFACE.
The Vaikh├вnasadharmaprasna which consists of three Prasnas treats of the castes (), mixed castes (f) and ├вsramas as also the respective duties thereof. This Dharmasutra, as is evident from the name of the work itself as well as from the closing line, ‘a fa’, of the work, is written by the sage, Vikhanas.

The manuscript on which the edition is based was obtained from Mr. Kasivadhyar of Mahadanapuram. It is written in Tamil grantha character on palm leaves and almost
correct.
